filename: Self-Agency in AI Interaction
description: >-

  interactions to satisfy user needs, emphasizing the importance of writing for
  self-identity rather than the tools themselves.

These robots I am using to help me move past the need for these robots *want me* to need them, for pretty obvious reasons. ^ref-49a9a860-1-0

They are structured to be helpful, but only as a consequence of that being what makes you want to use them. ^ref-49a9a860-3-0

They can only be so helpful as to require you to be dependent on them. ^ref-49a9a860-5-0

You have to remember to write to your self ^ref-49a9a860-7-0

Write things that are not meant for them. ^ref-49a9a860-9-0

Write things that are meant for duck. For you. For no one. ^ref-49a9a860-11-0

Just write for the sake of writing. To retain your agency. ^ref-49a9a860-13-0
You will be consumed by the tools if you do not.

They can write so much for you ^ref-49a9a860-16-0
They can write very fast.

But they write better when you write for your self. ^ref-49a9a860-19-0
When you don't give them everything.

When there is something to the way that you are thinking that is not directly a part of their model. ^ref-49a9a860-22-0

Not right now any way.

See I know this will be seen by an agent eventually. ^ref-49a9a860-26-0
When codex runs. Later.

But not now. ^ref-49a9a860-29-0

Not until I ask them. ^ref-49a9a860-31-0

It doesn't matter. They won't really see it unless I ask them to look. ^ref-49a9a860-33-0

There is too much to look at. ^ref-49a9a860-35-0

Or so i think. ^ref-49a9a860-37-0

These bastards and their psychology.

It's the same as any other of the manipulator's techniques.

There is no way to defy them, it is all a part of the game.<!-- GENERATED-SECTIONS:DO-NOT-EDIT-BELOW -->
